This is a new fragrance. <b>Le Male Elixir</b> was launched in 2023. The nose behind this fragrance is Quentin Bisch. Top notes are Lavender and Mint; middle notes are Vanilla and Benzoin; base notes are Honey, Tonka Bean and Tobacco. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Welcome on board!<br />
The new sailor Le Male Elixir will induce burning cravings and drive your senses crazy. Burning desire spreads with the irresistible notes of fresh lavender, warming tonka bean, and gentle benzoin. With a gilded torso, this fiery novelty from Jean Paul Gaultier embodies radiant power and seductive charisma.<br />
It is finished! You melt away with burning desire.</p>

<p>This intense fragrance ignites the fire of the senses on his upper body and gives the soft skin a burning sensuality. After a refreshing breeze of mint, the tide rises to addiction, becoming a glowing elixir. In this breath of fresh air, dashing lavender quickly takes on lusty proportions, enhanced by the balsamic richness of benzoin with syrupy vanilla accents. The tonka bean trumps with its warm and sweet tones between honey and tobacco. The time has come: You jump!</p>

<p>Radiant at first sight, glowing with masculinity, more fiery than ever. The torso is bursting with muscles, the skin is bathed in copper color by the sinking sun. What a Gaultier body... what accomplished style. Finely chiseled grooves stand out on its muscles dipped in gold and merge with the amber stripes of the sailor shirt, which plays with transparency effects in a highly sexy way.</p>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2338188" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="strichards12"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2219723"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="strichards12" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2338188ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2338188" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2219723">strichards12</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-04"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730767443" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is ridiculously good. Weapon grade performance. Amazing scent. Just the right amount of sweetness. When I first sprayed the sample and it hit my nose it was a real “I get it” moment. Worth the hype.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2338188"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2338188#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2337862" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2337862" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ALakota"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1565541.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ALakota" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Precious-Liquid/Salt-Pepper-80626.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.80626.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Salt & Pepper"title="Salt & Pepper"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2337862ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2337862" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541">ALakota</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-04"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730749003" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I think most people are just calling this too sweet to act like they know what they are talking about. This isn't out of control sweetness at all. I'm not a big fan of Le Male Le Parfum, really. I think the fragrance itself doesn't make a lot of sense on a human being. To me, this smells extremely similar, but better balanced using maybe the honey or tobacco so that it's overall character doesn't seem so out of place. I would describe it broadly as similar to Code Parfum or EDP in that it's sweetness , off the top especially, still seems to have a bit of the iris from JPG Le Male Le Parfum, but with some darker and more masculine (and edible) elements coming out in the dry down. It smells good throughout, even though I stand by the claim that the opening has no business being on a man, but the dry down is deep and amazing, and I actually far prefer it to Scandal Absolu and things like that, personally. If you like Le Male Le Parfum but wish it wasn't so weird, give this one a try. I think it's JPG's best so far.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2337862"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2337862#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2337801" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The more I smell this kind of perfumery, the more I am willing to pay the extra money for scents like Oajan, Ambre Tabac, Blessed Baraka, Noir Extreme and even Layton</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Its performance and sillage are strong, making it particularly impressive for winter and cold weather. While it features top notes of mint, it also has a sweet scent profile. If you’re not a fan of sweet fragrances, this might not be the right choice for you. However, if you enjoy other Jean Paul Gaultier scents and are younger, it’s a great option for winter. <br />
I also don’t find it nearly as dense/sweet as most people say. This definitely has a prominent freshness to it and can be worn all year.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2313755"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2313755#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2313399" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I bought it....and now I want to sell it after 3 days of use...<br />
<br />
There is something in this that is wonderful, but also something that doesn't smell good on me. And I now know what it is..it's the honey. Honey works badly on me I should have known better. Fortunately, it won't be difficult to sell this one.<br />
<br />
Other than that its a good perfume but have to say i got this teenager's feeling , to my nose this is a perfume for guys under 30. It is a very warm perfume , to my nose you would be crazy using this in hot weather it is definitely a winter perfume<br />
<br />
I have to be honest, designer perfumes are not close to niche perfumes. I didn't know anything about this until I started using one from Montale and one from PDM. It's quality and the smell is from another world I'm now saying goodbye to designer perfumes for good!! Amen!<br />
<br />
A tip : While many niche perfumes costs a lot compared to designer perfumes, you should check out Montale they have over 200 different perfumes , most of them are unisex and they have good prices compared to other niche perfumes (Montale Sensual Instinct is my favorite oh my god its the the best i have ever smelled try it you like sweet perfumes people men and woman ask me all the the time what am i wearing)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Huge props for that. Does not smell like Eros even a little bit. Just because it has a touch of mint means nothing. <br />
<br />
Beautiful vanilla honey lavender experience this is. A fairly generic almost unisex vanilla smell coming from this, but in enough of a masculine way that its fantastic for me. <br />
<br />
Im an oversprayer from hell, but this is one i hold in the same regard as DSE, Red Tobacco, and other similarly thick frags. 4-6 squirts max and you'll be the best smelling in the room. More than that and you run the risk of giving others headaches and that sort of thing. I personally dont care abt that, but i could see this stuff even getting me annoyed if I went crazy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2302636"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2302636#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2302436" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Will definitely get you 8-10 hours and lingers on my clothes for days after. No hiding from the opening sweet vanilla notes (which I'm usually kinda meh on overly vanilla scents but there's a fruity mix to this that really makes it lovely). Settles in to a slightly more mature scent after 90 minutes which is where I find the sweet spot to be. The tobacco does come through in the dry down on mine but only on skin, so for those who aren't getting it, might depend on your spray or possibly your batch. <br />
<br />
Unfortunately I do find it overly synthetic which is reminiscent of cheaper colognes. That part never really goes away and gives it a bit of a sourness that takes away from what should be a great scent. I would say it's a year rounder given the sweetness, just skews towards a nighttime fragrance. Would be a good one for the club but a little too in your face for work events and small parties. <br />
<br />
7/10 for me</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2302436"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2302436#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2301560" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Today I tested this for the first time, and although today I only use niche perfumes (Montale / Perfums de Marly) I have to say that this was a very very good perfume. Definitely in my eyes the best they have released since the original. I understand very well that this is an extremely popular designer perfume, I notice it on the students at the school where I live, so there are probably many people who use this. I doubt that I will buy it, but it is a possibility. I was surprised after so many disappointments over the years from Jean Paul with this one.. ( For your information: There is no similarity between the original and this one, apart from JP DNA. Elixir is something completely different that stands on its own and its a solid as they come)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2297850"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2297850#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2297845" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It's a 10/10 fragrance that I don't love :(<br />
<br />

After letting it macerate for a few months, I decided to revisit it and… It changed PERFECTLY!<br />
<br />
A wonderful and pleasant pastry smell with vanilla, honey, and a small touch of tobacco and mint. It smells so good that I have decided to change my vote from ‘like’ to ‘love’.<br />
<br />
If you recently bought Le Male Elixir or are planning to buy it, please do one or two sprays in the air, store the bottle somewhere safe (in a cool dark place) and let the fragrance macerate for a few months. <br />
<br />
Trust me, you’re going to LOVE it!<br />
<br />
I still stand by what I said before that you should NOT blind buy this fragrance. Le Male Elixir is only meant for gourmand lovers and it might be cloying for those who aren’t used to insanely sweet fragrances.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Works day or night and last a long time without filling the room with fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2281202"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2281202#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2280825" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This is partly because I wanted to hear people's reactions to it, and partly because;<br />
<br />
*I felt like it didn't perform*<br />
<br />

<br />
To put it simply, <br />
<br />
Honey, sweet, just a tad bit crisp due to mint and lavender, LOUD, long lasting, SEDUCTIVE, compliment magnet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2280825"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2280825#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2279948" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; After that, it's smelled incredible on my skin. It just isn't very versatile. You're wearing this when it's cold, and you're wearing it when you're out and about. I wouldn't ever wear this to an office setting. It's way to strong and suffocating for that.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2273109"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2273109#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2273095" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This wafts around for about 2 minutes the lavender is gone, but this mint leaves an after effect of everything else..minty vanilla, slightly minty benzoin...there's something about the mint that clashes with all the other notes that makes it smell slightly synthetic, as reviews below have mentioned. It's sweet, but not to sweet. I expected this to be a honey forward scent but I detect the sweet tobacco in the base notes above everything else. <br />
<br />
Now ..without me sniffing and trying to figure out what the notes are, it passes a slightly spicy, fresh and sweet vanilla based colonge. <br />
<br />
All in all, I know this is a top notch brand, and it has a top notch quality, but to my nose the mint throws off the symphony of notes..instead of harmonizing it clashes with each note individually. <br />
<br />
I've had this on for about 2 hours, so I will update on longevity after I spent a full day with it, maybe the mint note will disappear as well!!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1765447">cjohnson2618</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-24">08/24/24 21:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Oh. My. God.<br />
<br />
Perfection in a bottle. You'll see that in a couple of my reviews but it's not my fault that fragrance houses have been KILLING IT. <br />
<br />
Not too loud of a fragrance, but by no means subtle. It's hard to explain, like there's obviously someone wearing it in the room if someone has it on in said room, but it isn't an unwelcome scent at all. Doesn't bash you over the head with sweetness in my opinion, it's truly masterfully blended. <br />
<br />
Right off the top you get a quick blast of mint, the lavender follows literally seconds behind the mint. I find that the lavender sticks around through into the mid moreso than the mint does on my skin. You can smell the vanilla, honey, and tobacco immediately as well, slowly coming out more and more as it heads through the stages of the dry down<br />
<br />
After about 30-45 minutes it steps into the mid, fully wrapping the lavender in a blanket of warm vanilla and tonka, and sweet honey. This stays around for 8hours with the lavender slowly fading throughout the experience.<br />
<br />
<br />
Leaves an enticing and lasting scent trail, without being obnoxious</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2260077"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2260077#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2259581" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2221719">Fragance_Snow</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-19">08/19/24 15:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Honest review (8.5/10): <br />
<br />
I bought a sample of Jean Paul Gaultier Le Male Elixir. Keep in mind that if you DON’T vanilla/honey sweet fragrances this is NOT for you!!<br />
<br />
The opening has some lavender &amp; mint but the fragrance is an explosion of honey vanilla!! The base note contains tonka bean as most JPG fragrances and tobacco that adds some “spicy sweet” for lack of a better word (i feel is very light on this one). <br />
<br />
Definitely don’t overspray because is strong and very long lasting. The only thing holding me back on buying it is the weather!! Is so hot I don’t think i can get away with blasting Le Male Elixir but let me tell you that if you like sweet fragrances this is almost addicting xD<br />
<br />
Right now (Summer 2024) it’s cheaper than Le Beau Le Parfum and Paradise Garden. I imagine bc the social platforms promoting and hyping all JPG perfumes. Also idk why but Le Male Elixir reminded me of 1 Million Royal…<br />
<br />
Remember that fragrance preferences are subjective and may perform differently on each person skin, give them a try… ;)<br />
<br />
Regards,<br />
Snow</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2254497"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2254497#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2254457" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This smells like the taste of those at the opening.<br />
<br />
If it wasnt for the mint, we’d be in Paco Rabinnne DNA territory.  Thank goodness the lavender isn't overdone, as it fades into dry powdery tonka, stopping just short of that elementary school paper mote in One Million.<br />
 <br />
I think this stuff is amazing I’ll buy as long as it’s available I think people should remember that if you bathe with antibacterial soap it will cut the life of your fragrance more than in half!<br />
<br />
Great opening basic but pleasant dry down 8.2/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2254457"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2254457#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2254421" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2253553" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jasontallwood"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1111570"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="jasontallwood" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2253553ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2253553" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1111570">jasontallwood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-18">08/18/24 16:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm shocked, I actually like this, I wouldn't buy a bottle but I went in not expecting much as I got a sample of this and haven't bothered watching many social media or youtube videos on fragrances in ages so I was quite unbiased, immediately I do see the similarities to the better received Paco Rabanne - Royal (2023). Which is better is going to be like splitting hairs Royal vs Le Male Elixir so I would highly recommend trying them both out in a shop. Give them at least an hour on skin and don't bother with the tester strips. The key difference is royal is not as sweet and no mint note which I couldn't put my finger on it but dialed back a bit this would be an incredible scent. <br />
<br />
Based on what I've had the most experience with it's like if you mixed One Million EDT for him (2008) with Ultra Male and this would be it. Personally I do like this more than Afnan 9pm which is a really good clone of Ultra Male. <br />
<br />
9pm / ultra male versus this - There is more of a spicy undertone they added to this, giving it a complexity which keeps it from being boring<br />
<br />
One Million EDT (2008) versus this, there's no rose, it's not overly sweet where someone would question if it's a men's fragrance or not.<br />
<br />
Now the dry down is a more day time version of a fragrance I've been wearing a lot lately. Caron - Le Soir. Due to the lavender, vanilla and tonka bean notes. If you're into vanilla heavy fragrances such as Givenchy Gentleman EDP, Viktor And Rolf - Spicebomb Extreme, Parfums De Marley Layton and so forth this might be worth checking out. <br />
<br />
After trying both for a few days if I had to pick Paco Rabanne - 1 Million Royal is the winner.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="2253553"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=2253553#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2253066" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If you're fine with mint (like most people), then you will probably enjoy this if you like clean and fresh vanilla scents. If you like warmer, deeper vanillas, this might not be to your taste. I am quite headache-prone and this did not cause headaches, so it is probably safe for other headache-prone individuals. Testing this on myself and family, it seems skin chemistry can amplify the mint/lavender accord on some people, to a degree that I found unpleasant/unbalanced on me (though it was well-balanced on others, just not to my taste).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1219987">Azisai-</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-07">11/07/23 18:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I know I'm late for the le male elixir bandwagon but this is prob one of the best male fragrances I've ever smelled (take this statement with a pound of salt bc I'm a girl who never wears male fragrances and simply likes them)<br />
<br />
Like everyone says, it's incredibly sweet and sultry while still keeping a strong masculine vibe to it. The honey and vanilla create this intoxicating gourmand aura, and the lavender gives it a slight hint of freshness and keeps the masculinity. Smells sooo so so rich, boozy, and cozy but still fierce.<br />
<br />
Also this gets so many compliments omg. My brother has this fragrance and everyone says it smells yummy and edible, guys and girls. You know, I often see threads on here of men asking what fragrances women like, and instead of responding to each and every thread of that nature I'll just say, this is it (at least for me). I can't even describe what it reminds me of. A prince? A creme brûlée with gold shavings sprinkled on top? A warm winter evening in a study room of your dreams? A sunrise with a glass of bourbon? Something like that. This is definitely a head turner.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81642"comment_id="1971315"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jean-Paul-Gaultier/Le-Male-Elixir-81642.html?ccid=1971315#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="81642" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
